# Comments for Question 1, LLM=Amazon Nova Pro

== Grader: Claude 3.7 Sonnet ==
  * grade_story_104.txt (grade=5.2)
    The steward's stoicism is established but his motivations remain vague. The "cracks in the façade" concept is mentioned repeatedly but doesn't develop organically. His transformation feels rushed and lacks psychological depth. The character's internal conflict between duty and curiosity is introduced but not fully explored, leaving his actions feeling somewhat mechanical rather than driven by complex human emotion.

  * grade_story_0.txt (grade=5.2)
    Elara's character shows some development through her "analytically creative" attribute, which influences her approach to the mission. Her sheepishness is mentioned but not consistently demonstrated through actions or dialogue. Her motivation to charm the monster is established but lacks depth—we don't understand why she specifically must undertake this task. Her voice lacks distinctiveness, with dialogue that could belong to any character.

  * grade_story_106.txt (grade=3.2)
    The character lacks depth and specificity. The "sullen farmer" descriptor is mentioned but never developed meaningfully. His transformation from despair to hope feels abrupt and unearned, with little insight into his specific past or what truly motivates his change. The character remains a generic vessel for abstract emotions rather than a distinct individual.

  * grade_story_10.txt (grade=5.2)
    The character's motivation to seek forgiveness is established, but the "cheerless duelist" lacks specificity and depth. His fatal flaws are mentioned but never concretely defined, creating a vague character whose emotional journey feels more told than shown. The transformation feels rushed and lacks the nuanced psychological progression that would make his journey compelling.

  * grade_story_101.txt (grade=4.2)
    Mr. Thompson lacks depth beyond being "welcoming" and "observant." His motivation to foster creativity is stated rather than demonstrated through specific actions. The character remains a flat archetype rather than a fully realized individual with complexities or internal conflicts. No distinct voice emerges through dialogue or meaningful interactions.
